event = { 
	id = 3180010
	random = no 
	country = TUR

	name = "Britain withdraws support from the Balkan Pact"
	desc = "The Balkan Pact, of which Turkey was a part, was to a great extent a British-sponsored treaty to preserve the status quo in the Balkan region against further revisionism. Shortly after coming to power in London, the Mosley government reassed its foreign policy priorities and withdrew its support from the Balkan pact."
	style = 2 

	date = { day = 7 month = february year = 1933 } 
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1942 } 

	action_a = { 
		name = "Do we still need this pact?"
		command = { type = money value = 5 }
		command = { type = belligerence value = 1 }
		#command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 2 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
	} 
}

	}

	style = 2
	picture = "SCW_Soviet_Intervention"

	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

				NOT = { manpower = 20 }

		}
	}

		flag = EGYCoup
	}

		OR = {
			war = { country = ENG country = SOV }
			war = { country = ENG country = USA }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				war = { country = SYR country = ENG }

			}

	country = SUD

  	picture = "news_paper"

		flag = EGYCoup
		exists = EGY
	}

		OR = {
			AND = {
				war = { country = ENG country = SUD }
				war = { country = ENG country = EGY }
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { war = { country = ENG country = SUD } }
				NOT = { war = { country = ENG country = EGY } }
			}
		}
	}

		ai = yes
		flag = EGYCoup
		exists = EGY
		local_flag = AllDefense2
		OR = {
			AND = {
				war = { country = ENG country = SUD }
				war = { country = ENG country = EGY }
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { war = { country = ENG country = SUD } }
				NOT = { war = { country = ENG country = EGY } }
			}
		}
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

		ai_chance = 100
		name = "We must seek Arab unity!"

event = {
	id = 2003250
	random = no
	country = ENG
	save_date = yes

	name = "Major uprising in Cyprus"
	desc = "With Greek support, a large scale uprising has erupted in Cyprus against the British colonial government! Complicating the situation further, the local Turkish minority is also fighting back against the Greek rebels. Still, they are loyal to Turkey, not to us. The Britsh armed forces are overstreched and are unable to keep the situation under control."
	style = 2
  	picture = "news_paper"
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			war = { country = ENG country = GRE }
			AND = {
				exists = SOV
				year = 1942
			}
		}
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1944 }

	action = {
		name = "Curses!"
		command = { type = removeclaim which = 387 }
		command = { type = independence which = U39 value = 1 when = 1 }
		command = { type = removeclaim which = 388 }
		command = { type = independence which = CYP value = 1 when = 1 }
		command = { type = end_mastery which = U39 }
		command = { type = end_mastery which = CYP }
		command = { type = event which = 2400535 where = U39 when = 0 } #independence flag
		command = { type = event which = 2400535 where = CYP when = 0 } #independence flag
		
		command = { type = trigger which = 2003251 } #CYP
		command = { type = trigger which = 2003252 } #U39
		command = { type = event which = 2003256 where = U39 when = 5 }
		
	}
}
